SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT stories.id) FROM `stories` LEFT OUTER JOIN `story_texts` ON `story_texts`.`id` = `stories`.`id` LEFT OUTER JOIN `taggings` ON `taggings`.`story_id` = `stories`.`id` LEFT OUTER JOIN `tags` ON `tags`.`id` = `taggings`.`tag_id` LEFT OUTER JOIN `users` ON `users`.`id` = `stories`.`user_id` WHERE `stories`.`merged_story_id` IS NULL AND `stories`.`is_expired` = FALSE AND ((MATCH(stories.title) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE) OR MATCH(stories.description) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE) OR MATCH(story_texts.body) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE)))
SELECT stories.*, MATCH(stories.title) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE), MATCH(stories.description) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE), MATCH(story_texts.body) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE) FROM `stories` LEFT OUTER JOIN `story_texts` ON `story_texts`.`id` = `stories`.`id` WHERE `stories`.`merged_story_id` IS NULL AND `stories`.`is_expired` = FALSE AND ((MATCH(stories.title) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE) OR MATCH(stories.description) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE) OR MATCH(story_texts.body) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE))) ORDER BY ((MATCH(stories.title) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE)) * 2) + ((MATCH(stories.description) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE)) * 1.5) + (MATCH(story_texts.body) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE)) DESC LIMIT 20 OFFSET 0

SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT comments.id) FROM `comments` LEFT OUTER JOIN `users` ON `users`.`id` = `comments`.`user_id` LEFT OUTER JOIN `stories` ON `stories`.`id` = `comments`.`story_id` WHERE `comments`.`is_deleted` = FALSE AND `comments`.`is_moderated` = FALSE AND (MATCH(comment) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE))
SELECT comments.*, MATCH(comment) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE) AS rel_comment FROM `comments` WHERE `comments`.`is_deleted` = FALSE AND `comments`.`is_moderated` = FALSE AND (MATCH(comment) AGAINST('hi' IN BOOLEAN MODE)) ORDER BY rel_comment DESC LIMIT 20 OFFSET 0

SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367283' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:37:55 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367283' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:37:55 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:37:55.049040') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:37:55.049040') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30

SELECT DISTINCT hotness AS alias_0, `stories`.`id` FROM `stories` LEFT OUTER JOIN `taggings` ON `taggings`.`story_id` = `stories`.`id` LEFT OUTER JOIN `tags` ON `tags`.`id` = `taggings`.`tag_id` WHERE `stories`.`merged_story_id` IS NULL AND `stories`.`is_expired` = FALSE AND (score >= 0) ORDER BY hotness LIMIT 25
SELECT `stories`.`id` FROM `stories` LEFT OUTER JOIN `taggings` ON `taggings`.`story_id` = `stories`.`id` LEFT OUTER JOIN `tags` ON `tags`.`id` = `taggings`.`tag_id` WHERE `stories`.`merged_story_id` IS NULL AND `stories`.`is_expired` = FALSE AND (score >= 0) AND `stories`.`id` IN (441, 408, 409, 410, 411, 412, 413, 414, 415, 416, 417, 418, 419, 420, 360, 362, 363, 364, 365, 366, 367, 368, 369, 370, 371) ORDER BY hotness
SELECT `stories`.* FROM `stories` WHERE `stories`.`merged_story_id` IS NULL AND `stories`.`is_expired` = FALSE AND NOT (EXISTS (SELECT TRUE FROM `hidden_stories` WHERE (hidden_stories.story_id = stories.id) AND `hidden_stories`.`user_id` = 2)) AND NOT (EXISTS (SELECT TRUE FROM `taggings` WHERE (taggings.story_id = stories.id) AND `taggings`.`tag_id` IN (17, 70, 154, 156))) AND (score < 5) AND (created_at >= '2020-12-30 09:39:04.794742') AND `stories`.`id` NOT IN (441, 408, 409, 410, 411, 412, 413, 414, 415, 416, 417, 418, 419, 420, 360, 362, 363, 364, 365, 366, 367, 368, 369, 370, 371) ORDER BY stories.created_at DESC LIMIT 26 OFFSET 0

SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367284' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:40:26 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367284' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:40:26 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:40:26.187266') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30

SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367284' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:40:37 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367284' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:40:37 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:40:37.477668') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30

SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367284' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:42:44 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:42:44.085992') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30

SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367284' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:44:28 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367284' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:44:28 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:44:28.033588') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30

SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367284' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:44:48 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:44:48.756875') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30

SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367285' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:45:33 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:45:33.315628') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30

SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT stories.id) FROM `stories` LEFT OUTER JOIN `story_texts` ON `story_texts`.`id` = `stories`.`id` LEFT OUTER JOIN `taggings` ON `taggings`.`story_id` = `stories`.`id` LEFT OUTER JOIN `tags` ON `tags`.`id` = `taggings`.`tag_id` LEFT OUTER JOIN `users` ON `users`.`id` = `stories`.`user_id` WHERE `stories`.`merged_story_id` IS NULL AND `stories`.`is_expired` = FALSE AND ((MATCH(stories.title) AGAINST('new' IN BOOLEAN MODE) OR MATCH(stories.description) AGAINST('new' IN BOOLEAN MODE) OR MATCH(story_texts.body) AGAINST('new' IN BOOLEAN MODE)))
SELECT stories.*, MATCH(stories.title) AGAINST('new' IN BOOLEAN MODE), MATCH(stories.description) AGAINST('new' IN BOOLEAN MODE), MATCH(story_texts.body) AGAINST('new' IN BOOLEAN MODE) FROM `stories` LEFT OUTER JOIN `story_texts` ON `story_texts`.`id` = `stories`.`id` WHERE `stories`.`merged_story_id` IS NULL AND `stories`.`is_expired` = FALSE AND ((MATCH(stories.title) AGAINST('new' IN BOOLEAN MODE) OR MATCH(stories.description) AGAINST('new' IN BOOLEAN MODE) OR MATCH(story_texts.body) AGAINST('new' IN BOOLEAN MODE))) ORDER BY ((MATCH(stories.title) AGAINST('new' IN BOOLEAN MODE)) * 2) + ((MATCH(stories.description) AGAINST('new' IN BOOLEAN MODE)) * 1.5) + (MATCH(story_texts.body) AGAINST('new' IN BOOLEAN MODE)) DESC LIMIT 20 OFFSET 0

SELECT stories.*, MATCH(stories.title) AGAINST('aliquam' IN BOOLEAN MODE), MATCH(stories.description) AGAINST('aliquam' IN BOOLEAN MODE), MATCH(story_texts.body) AGAINST('aliquam' IN BOOLEAN MODE) FROM `stories` LEFT OUTER JOIN `story_texts` ON `story_texts`.`id` = `stories`.`id` WHERE `stories`.`merged_story_id` IS NULL AND `stories`.`is_expired` = FALSE AND ((MATCH(stories.title) AGAINST('aliquam' IN BOOLEAN MODE) OR MATCH(stories.description) AGAINST('aliquam' IN BOOLEAN MODE) OR MATCH(story_texts.body) AGAINST('aliquam' IN BOOLEAN MODE))) ORDER BY ((MATCH(stories.title) AGAINST('aliquam' IN BOOLEAN MODE)) * 2) + ((MATCH(stories.description) AGAINST('aliquam' IN BOOLEAN MODE)) * 1.5) + (MATCH(story_texts.body) AGAINST('aliquam' IN BOOLEAN MODE)) DESC LIMIT 20 OFFSET 0

SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367285' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:46:24 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367285' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:46:24 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:46:24.189272') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30

SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367285' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:46:47 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:46:47.586650') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30

SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367285' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:47:12 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367285' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:47:12 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:47:12.418334') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30

SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367285' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:47:38 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367285' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:47:38 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:47:38.771828') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30

SELECT `keystores`.* FROM `keystores` WHERE `keystores`.`key` = 'traffic:at:5367285' LIMIT 1 stddev(sum_flags) as stddev, sum(sum_flags) as sum, avg(sum_flags) as avg, avg(n_comments) as n_comments, count(*) as n_commenters from ( select sum(flags) as sum_flags, count(*) as n_comments from comments join users on comments.user_id = users.id where (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 03:48:19 -0600') and users.banned_at is null and users.deleted_at is null GROUP BY comments.user_id ) sums
SELECT  users.id, users.username, (sum(flags) - 0)/0 as sigma, count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) as n_comments, count(distinct if(flags > 0, story_id, null)) as n_stories, sum(flags) as n_flags, sum(flags)/count(distinct comments.id) as average_flags, ( count(distinct if(flags > 0, comments.id, null)) / count(distinct comments.id) ) * 100 as percent_flagged FROM `users` INNER JOIN `comments` ON `comments`.`user_id` = `users`.`id` WHERE `users`.`banned_at` IS NULL AND `users`.`deleted_at` IS NULL AND (comments.created_at >= '2020-12-09 09:48:19.454140') GROUP BY comments.user_id HAVING (n_comments > 4 and n_stories > 1 and n_flags >= 10 and percent_flagged > 10) ORDER BY sigma desc LIMIT 30
